The Dragon is the direct representation of Chinese Emperors. It is the most sacred among all Chinese mythical beasts. For this Chinese New Year we are releasing a collaboration between Imperial Taels and MJ Fresh using the Dragon as our design premise.

1. MJ Fresh x Imperial Taels MA-1 Bomber Jacketï¼šfeaturing a full Dragon embroidery on the back and dual IT/MJF side labels with double zippers. Limited to 180 jackets at 3600NTD. 
2. Imperial Taels x MJ Fresh Dragon Medallion necklace: Gilded with 18K gold coating and featuring a Dragon on the front and dual logo engravings on the back, paired with our custom 18K coated cuban link necklace and limited to 50 pieces for 3600NTD.

Releasing this Chinese New Year on February 11th at Taipei and Taichung MJ Fresh Stores and Imperial Taels Taipei East District store in limited quantities at 2pm. There will also be 10 Limited Edition box versions with a jacket and a medallion each for the special value price of 6800NTD. All boxes are individually numbered.

We fused these two iconic themes into a completely unique print that includes subtle nuances in the expression of its characters that include lust, envy and pride.
